
========== TEST 1: Basic Read/Write ==========
Core 0 read 0x100 L1 has it state=3 data=0xdeadbeef
Core 0 read 0x100 L3 has it state=2 data=0xdeadbeef
PASS expected=deadbeef got=deadbeef

========== TEST 2: Same Core Write Twice ==========
Core 0 read 0x100 L1 has it state=3 data=0x11111111
Core 0 read 0x100 L3 has it state=2 data=0x11111111
PASS expected=11111111 got=11111111

========== TEST 3: Cross-Core Read ==========
SNOOP: addr=0x200 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
PASS expected=cafebabe got=cafebabe

========== TEST 4: Write Contention ==========
SNOOP: addr=0x300 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x300 type=1 core_id=0 contains=1
Core 0 read 0x300 L1 has it state=0 data=0x11111111
Core 0 read 0x300 L3 has it state=0 data=0x11111111
SNOOP: addr=0x300 type=0 core_id=1 contains=1
PASS expected=22222222 got=22222222

========== TEST 5: Three Core Contention ==========
Core 0 writing 0x400 NOT IN ANY LEVEL
Core 1 writing 0x400 NOT IN ANY LEVEL
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=1 core_id=0 contains=1
Core 2 writing 0x400 NOT IN ANY LEVEL
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=0 core_id=1 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=1 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=1 core_id=1 contains=1
Core 0 read 0x400 L1 has it state=0 data=0xaaaaaaaa
Core 0 read 0x400 L3 has it state=0 data=0xaaaaaaaa
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=0 core_id=1 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=0 core_id=2 contains=1
Core 1 read 0x400 L1 has it state=0 data=0xbbbbbbbb
Core 1 read 0x400 L3 has it state=0 data=0xbbbbbbbb
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=0 core_id=2 contains=1
Core 2 read 0x400 L1 has it state=1 data=0xcccccccc
Core 2 read 0x400 L3 has it state=1 data=0xcccccccc
PASS core0 expected=cccccccc got=cccccccc
PASS core1 expected=cccccccc got=cccccccc
PASS core2 expected=cccccccc got=cccccccc

========== TEST 6: False Sharing ==========
Core 0 read 0x500 L1 has it state=3 data=0xaaaaaaaa
Core 0 read 0x500 L3 has it state=2 data=0xaaaaaaaa
Core 1 read 0x504 L1 has it state=3 data=0xaaaaaaaa
Core 1 read 0x504 L3 has it state=2 data=0xaaaaaaaa
PASS core0 expected=aaaaaaaa got=aaaaaaaa
PASS core1 expected=bbbbbbbb got=bbbbbbbb

========== TEST 7: Ping Pong ==========
SNOOP: addr=0x600 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x600 type=1 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x600 type=0 core_id=1 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x600 type=1 core_id=1 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x600 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x600 type=1 core_id=0 contains=1
Core 0 read 0x600 L1 has it state=0 data=0x3
Core 0 read 0x600 L3 has it state=0 data=0x3
SNOOP: addr=0x600 type=0 core_id=1 contains=1
PASS expected=00000004 got=4

========== TEST 8: Temporal Locality ==========
Core 0 read 0x700 L1 has it state=3 data=0x12345678
Core 0 read 0x700 L3 has it state=2 data=0x12345678
Core 0 read 0x700 L1 has it state=3 data=0x12345678
Core 0 read 0x700 L3 has it state=2 data=0x12345678

Core 0 read 0x700 L1 has it state=3 data=0x12345678
Core 0 read 0x700 L3 has it state=2 data=0x12345678
PASS expected=12345678 got=12345678

========== TEST 9: Read Then Write ==========
SNOOP: addr=0x800 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x800 type=1 core_id=1 contains=1
Core 1 read 0x800 L1 has it state=0 data=0xdead0000
Core 1 read 0x800 L3 has it state=0 data=0xdead0000
SNOOP: addr=0x800 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
PASS core1 first read expected=dead0000 got=dead0000
PASS core1 second read expected=dead1111 got=dead1111

========== TEST 10: Multiple Addresses ==========
Core 0 read 0x900 L1 has it state=3 data=0x11111111
Core 0 read 0x900 L3 has it state=2 data=0x11111111
Core 0 read 0x940 L1 has it state=3 data=0x22222222
Core 0 read 0x940 L3 has it state=2 data=0x22222222
Core 0 read 0x980 L1 has it state=3 data=0x33333333
Core 0 read 0x980 L3 has it state=2 data=0x33333333
PASS expected=11111111 got=11111111
PASS expected=22222222 got=22222222
PASS expected=33333333 got=33333333

========== TEST 11: Eviction ==========
SNOOP: addr=0x200 type=1 core_id=1 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x300 type=1 core_id=1 contains=1
Core 0 writing 0x400 L2 currentState=2
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=1 core_id=1 contains=1
SNOOP: addr=0x400 type=1 core_id=2 contains=1
Core 0 read 0x0 L3 has it state=2 data=0x1
PASS evicted line readable from L2, expected=1 got=1
Core 0 read 0x400 L1 has it state=3 data=0x5
Core 0 read 0x400 L3 has it state=2 data=0x5
PASS newest line still in L1, expected=5 got=5

========== TEST 12: Eviction + Cross-Core Snoop ==========
SNOOP: addr=0x0 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
PASS core1 read before eviction, expected=aaaa0001 got=aaaa0001
Core 0 writing 0x400 L2 currentState=3
Core 1 read 0x0 L1 has it state=2 data=0xaaaa0001
Core 1 read 0x0 L3 has it state=1 data=0xaaaa0001
PASS core1 still correct after core0 eviction, expected=aaaa0001 got=aaaa0001
SNOOP: addr=0x0 type=1 core_id=1 contains=1
Core 1 read 0x0 L1 has it state=0 data=0xaaaa0001
Core 1 read 0x0 L3 has it state=0 data=0xaaaa0001
SNOOP: addr=0x0 type=0 core_id=0 contains=1
PASS core1 sees updated value after invalidation, expected=bbbb0001 got=bbbb0001
Core 0 read 0x0 L1 has it state=1 data=0xbbbb0001
Core 0 read 0x0 L3 has it state=1 data=0xbbbb0001
PASS core0 reads own write, expected=bbbb0001 got=bbbb0001
